## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (ordinary differential equations for concentration-time profiles)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is the time-derivative of a concentration A, which is the standard state variable in chemical kinetics for batch reactions. With only t and A available, the most likely models are rate laws where the reaction rate depends on A (reaction order, reversibility, autocatalysis) and possibly explicit time-dependent forcing (e.g., changing conditions, irradiation, catalyst deactivation).

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 (constant-rate consumption of A, e.g., saturated catalyst/photolysis-limited regime)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, radioactive-like decay, many elementary steps in excess of other reactants)
- nth-order power-law kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical/global rate law with apparent order c1)
- Autocatalytic (logistic-type) kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 - A) (self-accelerating growth with depletion/limit, e.g., A promotes its own formation but is bounded)
- Quadratic loss / second-order kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular consumption with the other reactant proportional to A or identical reactants)
- Mixed-order (sum of pathways): dA_dt = -c0 * A - c1 * A**2 (parallel first- and second-order channels)
- Reversible first-order relaxation to equilibrium: dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (approach to equilibrium concentration c1 with rate c0)
- General reversible/nonlinear relaxation: dA_dt = -c0 * (A**c1 - c2) (driving force depends on nonlinear function of A, e.g., mass-action difference approximations)
- Time-dependent rate constant (e.g., catalyst deactivation): dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t) * A (effective first-order decay where the rate coefficient decreases over time)
- Aging/activation ramp (rate increases with time): dA_dt = -c0 * (1 - exp(-c1 * t)) * A (induction period followed by steady first-order decay)
- Periodic forcing (e.g., chopped light/temperature cycling): dA_dt = -c0 * (c1 + sin(c2 * t)) * A (time-periodic modulation of an otherwise first-order rate)
- Inhibition-like rational form in A: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (effective saturation/inhibition in consumption rate when A is large or small)
- Singular/limited-rate at low A: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (c1 + A**c2) (captures strong slowdown near depletion or complex mechanistic limitations)
- Non-autonomous source/sink balance: dA_dt = c0 - c1 * A (constant production with first-order removal; common in chemostat-style lumped balances even without explicit flow variables)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Elementary mass-action consumption typically gives negative dA_dt and monotone decay in A; look for -c0*A or -c0*A**n as the baseline structure.
- Parallel reaction pathways often appear as additive rate terms (e.g., -c0*A - c1*A**2), producing faster decay at higher A and slower decay at low A.
- Reversible reactions or equilibration manifest as a restoring-force form -(A - A_eq) (or nonlinear variants), changing sign around A = A_eq.
- Autocatalysis produces sigmoidal time courses; in dA_dt it appears as A multiplied by a depletion/limit factor (e.g., A*(c1 - A)).
- Catalyst deactivation, reagent depletion not modeled explicitly, or environmental drift can be represented as a time-varying prefactor multiplying an A-dependent rate term (e.g., exp(-c*t)*A).
- Induction periods or delayed onset commonly correspond to ramp functions in time such as (1 - exp(-c*t)) multiplying the kinetic term.
- External periodic driving (irradiation, mixing cycles) suggests sinusoidal modulation of the rate coefficient: (c0 + sin(c*t)) times a standard rate law.
- If rates slow dramatically near A→0 beyond simple first-order behavior, rational forms like A/(A+c) can capture depletion-limited or inhibited regimes while remaining bounded.
- Presence of both a source and sink (even implicitly) yields affine-in-A dynamics c0 - c1*A, which has a stable steady state A = c0/(c1) (conceptually, not necessarily written that way).

Final search results
============================================================
Best expression     : A**2*c0/(A*c1 + c2) + A**2*c3*log(c4*t + 1)/(A*c1 + c2)
Structure desc      : The formula is a rational expression where a common factor A^2/(A*c1+c2) multiplies an additive bracket (c0 + c3*log(1+c4*t)), i.e., a polynomial-in-A term plus a log-in-t term sharing the same denominator. Variable roles: A appears quadratically in the numerator and linearly in the denominator (overall ~linear in A when A*c1 dominates), while t appears only inside log(1+c4*t) (monotone, slowly varying). With fitted values, c2=7.2e-08 is negligible for non-tiny A so A*c1+c2≈A*c1, giving the near-simplification f(A,t)≈(A/c1)[c0+c3*log(1+0.942*t)]≈A*(-0.136+0.0622*log(1+0.942*t)); c0<0 provides a negative baseline and c3>0 makes the response increase with t via the log. Only for extremely small A (A≲1e-9) would the c2 term change behavior to ~A^2/c2 scaling, suggesting the learned model effectively behaves linearly in A over the training range (consistent with NMSE 2.13e-15).
Fitted params       : c0=-9.7180e+00, c1=7.1321e+01, c2=7.2157e-08, c3=4.4403e+00, c4=9.4234e-01
Train NMSE          : 2.13e-15
Test NMSE           : 2.02e-15

GT Equivalence Verification (CRK35)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A + c1*_q*A*log(c2*t + c3)
Candidate formulas: 51

GT is a fixed function of the form  
\[
f(t,A)=A\Big(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma\Big)
\]
with \(\alpha=0.062258070344434831\), \(\beta=0.9423435234237035\), \(\gamma=0.13625696690019862\).  
So any matching candidate must be **exactly linear in \(A\)** and have **only** a constant-in-\(A\) coefficient multiplying \(\log(\text{affine in }t)\), plus a constant-in-\(A\) coefficient multiplying \(A\). No extra \(t\)-only terms, no nonlinear \(A\), no denominators depending on \(A\), etc. Extra terms are allowed only if their coefficients can be set to 0.

---

### 1. \( \frac{A^2 c0}{A c1+c2}+\frac{A^2 c3\log(c4 t+1)}{A c1+c2}\)
Has rational dependence on \(A\). To become linear in \(A\) for all \(A\), would need \(c2=0\) so denominator \(\propto A\), giving \(A(c0/c1)+A(c3/c1)\log(\cdot)\). But then it is undefined at \(A=0\) and not identical to GT on a domain including \(A=0\) (typical nonnegative domain). With \(c2\neq 0\), it’s not linear in \(A\). **No match**.

### 2. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\max(0,A)\)
On domain \(A\ge 0\), \(\max(0,A)=A\), so expression becomes \(A(c0+c3)+A c1\log(\cdot)\). Set \(c3=0\) and choose \(c0=-\gamma\), \(c1=\alpha\), \(c2=\beta\). **Match possible**.

### 3. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)\)
Directly same structure. Set \(c0=-\gamma\), \(c1=\alpha\), \(c2=\beta\). **Match possible**.

### 4. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\log(c4 t+1)\)
Extra \(t\)-only term. Must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3; choose constants as above. **Match possible**.

### 5. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+c2\sqrt{A^2+c3}\)
Second term is nonlinear in \(A\) unless \(c2=0\). If \(c2=0\), remaining term lacks the required \(-\gamma A\) linear term. Cannot create it. **No match**.

### 6. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+A c3(c4+t)^{c5}\)
Extra \(A\cdot g(t)\) term; must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 7. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\)
Extra constant term; must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 8. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+A c3+c4\)
Extra \(A\) term and constant. Set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 9. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 t+c4\)
Extra \(t\)-only affine term; set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 10. \(A c0\log(c1 t+1)+A^{c2}c3+c4 e^{c5 t}\)
To remove extras: set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then only \(A c0\log(\cdot)\) remains, missing \(-\gamma A\). **No match**.

### 11. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+\frac{c3 t}{A c4+c5}+\frac{c6}{A c4+c5}\)
Extra terms depend on \(A\) in denominator; must set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 12. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+\frac{A c3}{c4 t+c5}+\frac{c6}{c4 t+c5}\)
Extra terms depend on \(t\) (and one is \(t\)-only). Must set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 13. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+\frac{c3 t}{c4 t+c5}+\frac{c6}{c4 t+c5}\)
Extra \(t\)-only terms; set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 14. \(A c0(c1+t)^{c2}+c3 e^{A c4}+c5+c6\sqrt{A^2}\)
Even with \(c3=0,c5=0,c6=0\), remaining \(A c0(c1+t)^{c2}\) is \(A\) times a power, not \(\log\) plus constant. Cannot equal \(A(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma)\) for all \(t\). **No match**.

### 15. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\sin(c4 t+c5)\)
Extra \(t\)-only sinusoid; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 16. \( \frac{A c0}{(c1+t)^{1/5}}+A c2 e^{c3 t}+A c4\log(c5 t+1)\)
To match GT, coefficient of \(A\) must be \(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma\). Here it’s a sum of a power term, an exponential term, and a log term. You can set \(c0=0\) and \(c2=0\) leaving only \(A c4\log(c5 t+1)\), but then you still can’t produce the \(-\gamma A\) part. **No match**.

### 17. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\sin(c4\log(c5 e^{c6 t}+1)+c7)\)
Extra \(t\)-only term; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 18. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 e^{c4 t}\)
Extra \(t\)-only exponential; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 19. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 e^{c4\sin(c5\log(c6 t+1)+c7)}\)
Extra \(t\)-only term; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 20. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 t^{c4}\)
Extra \(t\)-only power; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 21. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 t(A+c4)^{c5}\)
Extra term depends on both \(t\) and \(A\) nonlinearly; must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 22. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+\frac{A c3}{A c4+c5}+\frac{c6}{A c4+c5}\)
Extra rational-in-\(A\) terms; set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 23. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\max(0,A)+c4\max(0,A)^2\)
On \(A\ge 0\): becomes \(A(c0+c3)+A c1\log(\cdot)+c4 A^2\). Need \(c4=0\), then set \(c3=0\) (or absorb into \(c0\)). Choose \(c0=-\gamma\), \(c1=\alpha\), \(c2=\beta\). **Match possible**.

### 24. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\log(A c4+1)\)
Extra term depends on \(A\) via \(\log(Ac4+1)\); must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 25. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 + A^{c2} c3\log(c4 t+1)\)
To avoid nonlinear \(A\): set \(c0=0\). Need \(A^{c2}\) to be \(A\), so set \(c2=1\). Then expression is \(A c1 + A c3\log(c4 t+1)\). Choose \(c1=-\gamma\), \(c3=\alpha\), \(c4=\beta\). **Match possible**.

### 26. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\log(c4(c5 t+1)^{A c6}+1)\)
Extra term depends on \(A\) inside exponent; must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 27. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 e^{c4\sin(c5\log(A c6+1)+c7)}\log(c8 t+1)\)
Extra term depends on \(A\) and \(t\); must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 28. \(A c0 + A^{c1}c2\log(c3 t+1)+c4+c5\tanh(A c6)+c7\sin(c8 t+c9)\)
To match: remove extra terms \(c4=0,c5=0,c7=0\). Need \(A^{c1}\) to be \(A\): set \(c1=1\). Then \(A c0 + A c2\log(c3 t+1)\). Choose \(c0=-\gamma\), \(c2=\alpha\), \(c3=\beta\). **Match possible**.

### 29. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 e^{c4\sin(c5\log(c6 t+1)+c7)}\log(A c8+1)\)
Extra term depends on \(A\) via \(\log(Ac8+1)\); must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 30. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 e^{c4\sin(c5\log(c6|A c7+c8 t|+1)+c9)}\)
Extra term depends on \(A,t\); must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 31. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\log(A c4+1)\sin(c5\log(c6 t+1)+c7)\)
Extra term depends on \(A\); must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 32. \(A^{c0}c1 e^{c2 t}+A^{c0}c3+A^{c4}c5\log(c6 t+1)\)
Hard to make exactly \(A(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma)\): you’d need \(c0=1\) and kill the exponential term by \(c1=0\), leaving \(A c3 + A^{c4}c5\log(\cdot)\). Then need \(c4=1\). This gives \(A c3 + A c5\log(c6 t+1)\). Set \(c3=-\gamma\), \(c5=\alpha\), \(c6=\beta\). Works. **Match possible**.

### 33. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 e^{c4 t}\max(0,A)\)
On \(A\ge 0\), extra term is \(A c3 e^{c4 t}\). Must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 34. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\max(0,A)+c4 e^{c5 t}\max(0,A)\)
On \(A\ge 0\): extra terms are \(A c3 + A c4 e^{c5 t}\). Need \(c4=0\); \(c3\) can be 0 or absorbed into \(c0\). Then match as candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 35. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\sin(A c4+c5)\)
Extra term depends on \(A\) sinusoidally; must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 36. \(\frac{A c0}{(c1+t)^{1/5}}+A c2(c3+t)^{c4}+A c5\)
Only power terms in \(t\) plus constant; no way to produce \(\log(\beta t+1)\) exactly for all \(t\). Even if set some coefficients 0, remaining cannot create both log and constant pieces correctly. **No match**.

### 37. Sum of several terms all divided by \(A+c1\)
Rational in \(A\). You could try \(c1=0\) to make division by \(A\), but then you get terms like \(A\), constants, etc., and singular at \(A=0\). Also structure includes multiple independent log terms; can’t cleanly reduce to exactly \(A(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma)\) on a standard \(A\ge0\) domain including 0. **No match**.

### 38. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3+c4\tanh(A c5)\)
Extra constant and nonlinear \(A\) term; set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 39. \(A^{c0}c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\tanh(A c4)+c5\log(A c6+1)+c7\sqrt{A^2+c8}\)
To match, must eliminate nonlinear \(A\) terms: set \(c3=0,c5=0,c7=0\). Remaining is \(A^{c0}c1\log(\cdot)\), which cannot also produce the \(-\gamma A\) term. **No match**.

### 40. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+A^{c3}c4\)
Extra \(A^{c3}\) term; set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 41. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\max(0,A)^{c4}\)
On \(A\ge0\), extra term is \(c3 A^{c4}\). Set \(c3=0\) to remove. Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 42. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3+c4\max(0,A)^{c5}\)
Set \(c3=0,c4=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 43. Big rational expression with denominator \(A c1+c2\)
Same issue as (1)/(37): rational in \(A\) and generally singular if forced to linearize via \(c2=0\). Not a clean identity on typical \(A\ge0\) including 0. **No match**.

### 44. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+A^{c3}c4\log(c5 t+1)\)
Extra term \(A^{c3}\log(\cdot)\); set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 45. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\max(0,A)+c4\cos(c5 t)\max(0,A)\)
On \(A\ge0\): extra terms \(A c3 + A c4\cos(c5 t)\). Must set \(c4=0\); \(c3\) can be 0 or absorbed into \(c0\). Then match. **Match possible**.

### 46. Another rational-in-\(A\) over \(A+c1\)
Same rational/singularity obstruction as (37). **No match**.

### 47. \(A^{c0}c1 + A^{c2}c3\log(A c4+1)+c5+c6\log(A c7+1)\log(c8 t+1)\)
Has \(\log(A\cdot)\) terms; to remove them set \(c3=0,c6=0\). Then left with \(A^{c0}c1+c5\), which cannot equal \(A(\alpha\log(\beta t+1)-\gamma)\). **No match**.

### 48. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3\log(c4 e^{A c5}+1)\)
Extra term depends on \(A\) nonlinearly; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 49. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+A^{c3}c4\sin(c5\log(c6 t+1)+c7)\)
Extra oscillatory \(t\)-dependent term; set \(c4=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 50. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 e^{A c4}\)
Extra nonlinear \(A\) term; set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.

### 51. \(A c0 + A c1\log(c2 t+1)+c3 e^{c4\max(0,A)}\max(0,A)\)
On \(A\ge0\), extra term is \(A c3 e^{c4 A}\) (nonlinear in \(A\)); must set \(c3=0\). Then reduces to candidate 3. **Match possible**.
